What in the world is wrong with this thing...
这东西到底哪里有问题... 
You see the scientist struggle with a computer that is rapidly blinking and turns off.
你看到科学家在努力修理\n一台快速闪烁并机的电脑。
There's something up with this computer. If only I had a 多边兽 to work it out...
这电脑有问题。如果我有\n一个多边兽就能解决了... 
Actually hey, could you go and get me one please?
实际上，\n你能帮我去找一个吗？
I've been needing one anyways, since I work with computers. So please do a trade with me for it, I'll figure out what to get you for it.
我一直在需要一个因为我工作需要。\n所以请和我交易，我会想出给你什么回报。
Well no rush, maybe it'll mysteriously start working again... and yes, I turned it off and on again.
不急，也许它会突然又开始工作了... \n是的，我已经尝试过关机再开机了。
Ah, alright. Check again with me if you change your mind.
吧，如果你改变主意，\n再来找我。
Thank you, let's get it traded.
谢谢，我们开始交易吧。 
You trade over the 多边兽. It enters the computer, and a buzzing sound is heard as a 脱壳忍者 flies out.
你把多边兽交易了。它进入了电脑，\n发出嗡嗡的声音，一个脱壳忍者飞了出来。
You catch it to prevent it from causing any other trouble.
你抓住它，防止它再引起其他麻烦.
What the- it was actually a bug in there? Well damn, okay. You can keep it I guess, the computer is working perfectly.
这是——里面竟然有一个虫子？\n好吧，你把它留下吧，电脑运行得很好。
Thank you for this!
谢谢你！

目标覆盖着一层粉末，如果它使用火系技能，就会引发爆炸并受到伤害。
The user marks the target as eternal prey, leeching it.
使用者将目标标记为永恒的猎物，吸取它的精血。
The user launches steel bombs that stick to the target. Can't miss and skips protections.
使用者发射的钢制炸弹会粘在目标上。不会错过并且无视防护。
The user generates an intense magnetic connection between it and the target, striking it without fail.
使用者在自身和目标之间产生强烈的磁性连接，无一例外地击中目标。
Attacks while destroying the terrain. This move fails in the absence of a terrain.
在破坏地形的同时进行攻击。如果没有地形，这个动作将失败。
The user breathes a pheromonal nerve-chilling agent. This move is also Ice-type.
使用者呼出一种含有费洛蒙的神经麻痹剂。这个技能也是冰属性。
The user attacks the foe with a bursting flame. It also damages Pokémon next to the target.
使用者使用爆发的火焰攻击敌人，同时也会伤害到目标旁边的宝可梦。
The user envelops itself in a veil made of water. It regains 1/8 of its HP on every turn.
使用者把自己包裹在水制成的面纱中。每回合回复自身最大生命值的1/8。
Strikes the target with lunar tides, then summons rain for five turns.
用月潮打击目标，然后在五回合内召唤雨水。
The user plays a pleasant melody that lulls the target into a deep sleep.
使用者播放一段悦耳的旋律，使目标进入深度睡眠。
For five turns, Grass-type moves are boosted, and grounded Pokémon restore HP every turn.
在五回合内，草系技能提升，地面的宝可梦每回合恢复体力。
The user scatters a big cloud of sleep-inducing dust around the target.
使用者在目标周围撒出一团诱导睡眠的灰尘。
The user scatters a cloud of paralyzing powder. It leaves the target numb.
使用者撒出一团麻痹粉。它使目标失去行动能力。
After slashing, it returns to switch with a party Pokémon. Critical hits land more easily.
挥砍之后，它会返回并与一只队伍中的宝可梦交换。更容易出现暴击。
A sweet scent that lowers the foe's evasiveness. It also lures wild Pokémon if used in grass, etc.
一种甜美的香气，能降低敌人的闪避率。如果在草丛中使用，还可以引诱野生宝可梦
For five turns: Electric attacks are boosted and grounded Pokémon can't sleep or be numbed.
持续五回合：电系攻击提升，地面系宝可梦无法睡眠或被麻痹。
Attacks with electric voltage rising from the ground. Power doubles on Electric Terrain.
地面电压攻击。在电力地形上，力量翻倍。
This turn, all Enemies attacks becomes Electric-type and can only target the user.
这次，所有敌人的攻击都会变成电系，并且只能以使用者为目标。
Attacks with its psychic power. Power increases and damages all opponents on Psychic Terrain.
使用念力进行攻击。在念力地形上，力量会增加并伤害所有对手。
The user employs hypnotic suggestion to make the target fall into a deep sleep.
使用者使用催眠暗示使目标进入深度睡眠。
If the foe knows any move also known by the user, the foe is prevented from using it.
如果目标知道使用者也会的招式，目标将无法使用该招式。
The user distracts the target by bending a spoon. It lowers the target's accuracy.
使用者通过弯曲勺子来分散目标的注意力，降低目标的命中率。
The user senses the foe's movements with its mind to ensure its next attack does not miss the foe.
使用者用心灵感应目标的动作，以确保下一次攻击不会错过目标。
Enables the user to hit a Dark type with any type of move. It also enables the user to hit an evasive foe.
使使用者可以使用任何类型的招式攻击黑暗类型。它还使使用者能够攻击回避的敌人。
For five turns, Psychic-type moves are boosted, and priority moves fail.
在五回合内，超能属性的招式威力提升，且先制招式无法使用。
The user makes the target float with its psychic power. The target is easier to hit for three turns.
使用者用念力让目标飘浮起来。目标在三回合内更容易被击中。
The foe is attacked with a blast of absolute-zero cold. The target instantly faints if it hits.
敌人被绝对零度的寒冷冲击。如果打中，目标会立刻晕倒。
The user dismisses the target, forcing it to switch out. Always goes last.
使用者赶走目标宝可梦，强制其替换。总是最后一个行动。
Darkness rolls over the field, damaging all other Pokémon, ending weather, and healing statuses.
黑暗覆盖全场，伤害所有其他宝可梦，结束天气并治愈状态。
For five turns, Fairy-type moves are boosted, and grounded Pokémon can't be burned/poisoned.
在五回合内，妖精属性的招式得到提升，地面的宝可梦不会被烧伤/中毒。
The user attacks with the power of the moon, guaranteeing a critical hit on foes with boosted stats.
使用者使用月亮的力量进行攻击，对状态提升的敌人必定造成暴击。
Attacks nearby enemies. Deals 50% more in moonglow. User loses 50% max HP.
攻击附近敌人。在月光下伤害提高50%。使用者最大生命值降低50%。
This move exists just to showcase the PBS Extensions system.
这个动作只是用来展示 PBS 扩展系统。

An item to be held by a Pokémon. The user gets three abilities, but its stats are cut by 10%.
宝可梦携带物品。使用者获得三个技能，但其能力值降低10%。
A held item. When a foe raises their stats, the herb is consumed to reset their stats.
宝可梦携带物品。当对手提升能力值时，该草药会被消耗以重置对手的能力值。
Heals your whole team a limited number of times. Restocked at PokéCenters and after resting.
可有限次数治愈你的整支队伍。在宝可梦中心或休息后可重新补充。
A wisp of ideas with infinite potential. Use it on a Pokémon to teach any one of their legal moves.
灵感的微光。对宝可梦使用，可教会其任何一个合法技能。
An ancient horn. Sound it to call 3 rare Pokémon to battle you. Recharged by walking in encounter zones.
古老的号角。吹响它以召唤三只稀有宝可梦与你对战。通过在遭遇区域行走来重新充能。
A glamorous steel card. While holding it, all vendors cost 10% less and Poké Marts have extra items.
华丽的钢制卡片。持有它时，所有商贩的价格降低10%，且宝可梦商店会有额外商品。
A vessel for negative emotions. If you perfectly defeat enough route or gym trainers, it will grant you rewards.
负面情绪的容器。完美击败足够的路线或道馆训练家后，它会给予你奖励。

一张色彩斑斓的钥匙卡。它能解锁甜蜜岩港灯塔的电梯。
A spray-type medicine. It heals all the status problems of a single Pokémon.
一种喷雾型药品。它能治愈一只宝可梦的所有状态异常。
An item to test the PBS Extensions feature. It can be sold to shops for $1.
一个用于测试PBS扩展功能的物品。它可以以1美元的价格卖给商店。

At the end of each turn, if in rainstorm, each Pokémon not immune to rainstorm has their defensive stats lowered by 1 step.
每个回合结束时，若处于暴雨中，不免疫暴雨的宝可梦防御降低1级。
Takes 30% less damage in eclipse, except in total eclipse.
在日食时受到的伤害减少30%，完全日食除外。
When this Pokémon becomes statused, its Attack is raised by three steps.
当宝可梦陷入异常状态时，其攻击提升3级。
Immune to Ground-type moves. Takes 20% less damage in sandstorm.
免疫地面属性招式。在沙暴中受到的伤害减少20%。
Takes 25% less damage in a rainstorm.
在暴雨中受到的伤害减少25%。
Doubles Sp. Def in sunshine.
在晴朗天气下，特防翻倍。
If the Pokémon witnesses a total eclipse, it gets to move twice that turn.
如果宝可梦目睹了完全日食，则该回合可以行动两次。
Raises each stat by two steps when a total eclipse happens.
当完全日食发生时，所有能力提升2级。
On the first turn, its attacks cause the target to flinch.
首回合，其攻击会使目标畏缩。
Doubles Defense in rainstorm.
在暴雨中，防御翻倍。
Changes the weather to ring eclipse, which heralds the total ring eclipse. Lingers for 3 turns after leaving.
将天气变为环食，预示着完全环食的到来。离开后效果持续3回合。
Boosts Attack by 20% in hail, or 40% if also below half health.
在冰雹中，攻击提升20%，若生命值低于一半，则提升40%。
Boosts Speed by 50% in rainstorm. Doubles random added effect chance in rainstorm.
在暴雨中，速度提升50%。在暴雨中，随机附加效果的发生概率翻倍。
At the end of each turn, if in sunshine, each Pokémon not immune to sunshine has their defensive stats lowered by 1 step.
每个回合结束时，若处于晴朗天气下，不免疫晴朗天气的宝可梦防御降低1级。
When a total eclipse occurs, heals for 50% max HP and uses Heal Bell.
当完全日食发生时，回复最大生命值的50%并使用治愈铃声。
Boosts Speed by 50% in rainstorm. Can't miss during rainstorm.
在暴雨中，速度提升50%。在暴雨中，攻击必定命中。
Lays an electrical hazard around the opponent when its HP is lowered below half.
当生命值低于一半时，在对手周围布置电气场地。
The Pokémon starts as a very convincing Pikachu!
宝可梦初始形态为非常逼真的皮卡丘！
Adapts the move's type to ensure it is super-effective against the target.
改变招式属性以确保对目标效果绝佳。
Adapts the move's type to ensure it is truly super-effective against the target.
改变招式属性以确保对目标必定效果绝佳。
Adapts the move's type to maximize effectiveness while accounting for the immunities.
改变招式属性以在考虑免疫性的同时最大化效果。
Adapts the move's type to maximize damage against the target.
改变招式属性以最大化对目标的伤害。
This ability exists just to showcase the PBS Extensions system.
此特性仅用于展示PBS扩展系统。
Makes foes unable to use priority attacks.
使对手无法使用优先度招式。
Sets Fairy Terrain for five turns when hit by an attack.
受到攻击时，设置5回合的妖精场地。
Doubles the Speed of kicking moves.
踢击类招式的速度翻倍。
Doubles the speed of recoil moves.
反作用力招式的速度翻倍。
Sets Grassy Terrain for five turns when hit by an attack.
受到攻击时，设置5回合的青草场地。
Upon entry in sunshine, regenerates its used berry.
在晴朗天气下入场时，恢复已使用的树果。

Wild Pokémon don't give experience in Pokémon Tectonic.
在宝可梦Tectonic中，野生宝可梦不会给予经验。
If you encounter a Pokémon you don't want, run away. It's guaranteed!
如果你遇到了不想要的宝可梦，逃跑吧。这是有保证的！
For example, healing at a Pokémon Center triggers this.
例如，在宝可梦中心治疗时会触发此效果。
There's a shortcut key(F) to instantly mount the bicycle while walking.
有一个快捷键（F），可以在行走时立即骑上自行车。
Individual Pokémon have unique Traits, Likes, and Dislikes.
每只宝可梦都有独特的特性、喜好和厌恶。
To customize your stats, adjust Style Points in any PokéCenter.
要自定义你的属性，请在任何宝可梦中心调整风格点。
Many type matchups were changed in Pokémon Tectonic.
在《宝可梦：地壳变动》中，许多属性克制关系发生了变化。
Check the 甜竹竹。 or the Battle Guide to learn these changes.
查看甜竹竹或战斗指南以了解这些变化。
The last 5 boxes of the PC are donation boxes.
PC的最后5个盒子是捐赠盒。
Pokémon placed in these boxes can never be withdrawn.
放入这些盒子的宝可梦永远无法取回。
In repayment, you get candy equal to their lifetime EXP earnings.
作为回报，你将获得与他们一生中获得的经验值相等的糖果。

You win a battle when all enemy Pokémon faint: reach 0 health points. You lose a battle if that happens to any of your Pokémon. Fainted Pokémon will revive in 7 turns.
你赢得战斗当所有敌方宝可梦倒下：生命值降至0。如果你的任何一只宝可梦发生这种情况，你就会输掉战斗。倒下的宝可梦将在7回合后复活。
Pokémon are healed after a trainer battle. You can heal your Pokémon at PokéCenters between battles. You can often use the Aid Kit instead to save on traveling time.
宝可梦在训练师战斗后会恢复。你可以在战斗之间的宝可梦中心治疗你的宝可梦。你通常可以使用援助套装来节省旅行时间。
Power Points, or PP, is a number which limits how many times a move can be used. Healing at a PokéCenter, after a trainer battle or with the Aid Kit restores PP.
技能点数（PP）是一个限制技能使用次数的数值。在宝可梦中心、训练师战斗后或使用援助套装治疗时，可以恢复PP。
The three main methods of acquiring Pokémon are using DexNav, catching them from the wild, and receiving them from other Trainers through gifts or trades.
获取宝可梦主要有三种方法：使用DexNav、从野外捕捉以及通过其他训练师的赠送或交换获得。
Use the DexNav to get information on which Pokémon are available where you are.
使用DexNav来获取你所在位置可获得的宝可梦信息。
Stat steps start at 0, and can increase up to +12 (4x) and down to -12 (.25x). Stat steps usually are reset if you swap the Pokémon out or it faints.
属性等级从0开始，可以增加至+12（4倍）或降低至-12（0.25倍）。如果你将宝可梦换下或它倒下，属性等级通常会重置。
Abilities are special powers that Pokémon can have based on their species. Most Pokémon can have 2 possible abilities. All abilities activate in battle or on field.
特性是宝可梦根据其种类可能拥有的特殊能力。大多数宝可梦可能拥有两种特性。所有特性都在战斗或场上激活。
Abilities do a wide variety of different things. Understanding your team's abilities is important to winning.
特性具有多种多样的不同效果。了解你团队的特性对于获胜至关重要。
Check your Pokémon's summary to see what displaying ability they have. Use the 甜竹竹。 to read about the abilities of enemy Pokémon during battle.
查看你的宝可梦概要以了解其展示的特性。在战斗中，使用甜竹竹来阅读敌方宝可梦的特性。
A Pokémon's displaying ability is one of the two its species can have, randomly chosen when you get it. You can use Ability Capsules to swap to the other.
宝可梦的展示特性是其种类可能拥有的两种特性之一，在你获得它时随机选择。你可以使用特性胶囊来切换到另一种特性。
Status Conditions are removed when you heal at the PokéCenter, after a trainer battle or when you use the Aid Kit.
当你在宝可梦中心治疗、训练师战斗后或使用援助套装时，状态异常会被移除。
Certain abilities prevent critical hits against that Pokémon. The Lucky Chant effect and the Strategist tribe bonus also protect their side from critical hits.
某些特性可以防止对该宝可梦造成会心一击。幸运咒语效果和策略家部落加成也可以保护其所在方免受会心一击。
How to win?
如何获胜？

What is Move Mentoring?
什么是招式传授？
I'm the Mentor Coordinator. How can I help?
我是传授协调员。我能怎么帮你？
I help your Pokémon to teach each other moves!
我帮助你的宝可梦互相传授招式！
Pokémon can teach moves they know, moves they used to know, and moves earlier on their level up learnset.
宝可梦可以传授它们知道的招式、曾经知道的招式以及升级学习列表中较早的招式。
Any Pokémon in your party or in your PC can be a mentor.
你队伍中或PC里的任何宝可梦都可以成为传授者。
Pokémon can be taught any moves on their Other Moves list.
宝可梦可以学习它们其他招式列表中的任何招式。

What are Style Points?
什么是风格点？
I'm the Style Points adjuster. How can I help?
我是风格点调整器。我能怎么帮你？
Style Points are numbers which have an effect on your Pokemon's stats.
风格点是影响你宝可梦属性的数值。
Pokemon start with 10 Style Points in each of their stats.
宝可梦每项属性初始有10个风格点。
To add Style Points to a stat, you have to remove them from another.
要给某个属性增加风格点，必须从另一个属性中移除。
Investing into Attack and Sp. Atk is extra efficient: they go up at the same time!
投资于攻击和特攻特别高效：它们会同时提升！
Each stat's Style Points value can go as low as 0, and can go as high as 20.
每个属性的风格点值可以低至0，高至20。
A Pokemon's Style Point total never changes, but Style Points give bigger stat bonuses at higher levels.
宝可梦的风格点总数永不改变，但风格点在更高等级时提供的属性加成更大。
